  let rec common_divisors_aux n1 n2 n3 =

 (* Write a  function to find the sum of common divisors of two given numbers. *)
let common_divisors n1 n2 =
  let rec common_divisors_aux n1 n2 n3 =
    if n1 = n3 then n2
    else if n2 = n3 then n1

 (* Write a  function to find the sum of common divisors of two given numbers. *)

  let rec common_divisors_aux n1 n2 n3 =
